# MS932 <-> UTF-8 Conversion Table
#
# This file contains a byte-level mapping table between Microsoft code page
# 932 (MS932 / Windows-31J) and UTF-8.
#
# Each line describes a single character mapping and consists of four fields:
#
#   1. MS932 byte sequence
#      The byte sequence used in MS932 encoding.
#
#   2. UTF-8 byte sequence
#      The UTF-8 byte sequence representing the same character.
#
#   3. UTF-8 -> MS932 conversion result
#      The byte sequence obtained when the UTF-8 character is converted
#      back to MS932 using standard Windows conversion rules.
#
#   4. Comment
#      A short description of the character category or special notes.
#
# Byte values are written in hexadecimal without prefixes.
# Multi-byte sequences are written as concatenated hexadecimal bytes.
# Columns are separated by whitespace.
#
# Character coverage:
# This table includes displayable characters and only a minimal set of
# control codes that are commonly used in text files (such as TAB, LF, and CR).
# Other control codes are intentionally omitted.
#
# Note on round-trip conversion:
# In some cases the value in column 3 differs from column 1.
# This happens when multiple MS932 code points correspond to the same
# Unicode character. When converting from UTF-8 back to MS932,
# Windows selects a canonical MS932 code point, which may not be the
# same as the original byte sequence.
#
# This table therefore allows detection of characters that do not
# preserve their original byte sequence after a
# MS932 -> UTF-8 -> MS932 round-trip conversion.
#
# This table is intended for:
#   - testing MS932 <-> UTF-8 conversions
#   - validating encoding implementations
#   - detecting characters that change during round-trip conversion
#
# Character categories appearing in comments include:
#   - US-ASCII
#   - Half-width Katakana
#   - Full-width Characters
#   - NEC special characters
#   - NEC selected IBM extensions
#   - IBM extensions
#
# Note:
# MS932 is a superset of Shift_JIS used on Microsoft Windows and includes
# several vendor-specific extensions.
#
